This is a list of  counties in Icon CK3.png Crusader Kings III.


Contents
1	See also
There are currently 3476 counties in the game.

This list was generated by parsing game data, due to the amount of information there is no way to guarantee no county has incorrect info.

Some duchy buildings like Theodosian Walls (Byzantion) and Aurelian Walls (Roma) are not included as special buildings in their respective county entries by design.

A couple of special buildings are only available with the DLC Medieval Monuments.png Medieval Monuments DLC.

Specific counties in the game located within Administrative Realms that have a Culture with the Cultivated Sophistication Tradition will have starting Development numbers higher than that shown in the below table.*

Hegemonies are intentionally not on this table to avoid expanding horizontally.

List of duchies

Please help with verifying or updating older sections of this article.
At least some were last verified for version 1.18.

This article is for the PC version of Crusader Kings 3 only.

Nav top.png
Crusader Kings III
List of Titles
Overview
County.png Counties
Duchy.png Duchies
Kingdom.png Kingdoms
Empire.png Empires
Hegemony.png Hegemonies
This is a list of  duchies in Icon CK3.png Crusader Kings III. There are currently 911 duchy titles with land in the game.

This list was generated by parsing game data, due to the amount of information there is no way to guarantee no duchy has incorrect info.

Some duchy buildings like Theodosian Walls (Byzantion) and Aurelian Walls (Roma) are not included as special buildings in their respective duchy entries by design.

A few special buildings are only available with the DLC Medieval Monuments.png Medieval Monuments or DLC Holy Buildings.png Holy Buildings DLC.

Hegemonies are intentionally not on this table to avoid expanding horizontally.

Tögsköl Khanate	Roma	Possibly Italy, Romagna, Sardinia, Sicily, Venice	0-5	Collapse of the Mongol Empire in the region of Western Europe	0-71	e_togskol_khanate	
Uyghur Khanate	Karabalgasun	None (titular title)	0		0	e_uyghur_khanate	
White Horde	Praha	Possibly Bavaria, Bohemia, Great Moravia, Hungary, Moldavia, Wallachia	0-6	Collapse of the Mongol Empire in the region of Eastern Europe	0-134	e_white_horde

List of hegemonies
Jump to navigationJump to search
Please help with verifying or updating older sections of this article.
At least some were last verified for version 1.18.

This article is for the PC version of Crusader Kings 3 only.

Nav top.png
Crusader Kings III
List of Titles

Empire.png Empires
Hegemony.png Hegemonies
This is a list of  Hegemonies in Icon CK3.png Crusader Kings III.


All hegemonies after they were formed. Note that Dar al-Islam will include a second empire title, Khaganate can be larger if the steppes were expanded, and Dar al-Islam, Western Roman Empire and Eastern Roman Empire can be larger if other empires were held when the hegemony was created.
Hegemony	Empires	Capital	 Decision	Notes
China	
Jingyang
Liangyi
Lingnan
Yongliang
Zhongyuan
Jingzhao in 867
Bianzhou in 1066
Hangzhou in 1178
Already present	
Always uses the owner's dynasty name regardless of game settings
If the DLC All Under Heaven.png All Under Heaven DLC is installed the title unlocks additional mechanics:
Can only be destroyed and recreated via the Dynasty Cycle situation
Unlocks a large number of great projects
Uses the Grand Secretariat diarchy
Tributary system is expanded
Unlocks two additional laws if government remains  Celestial
Uses a different council if government remains  Celestial
India	
Deccan Empire
Pracya
Rajasthan
No	Become Chakravarti	
Dar al-Islam	
Arabian Empire
Any empire held when the decision was taken
Mecca	Establish the Dar al-Islam	Becomes the head of faith title for all Muslim faiths that consider the faith of the ruler taking the decision Righteous or Astray
Roman Empire	
Italia
Any empire held when the decision was taken
Roma if done by Italia or Holy Roman Empire
Byzantion if done by Byzantine Empire
Restore the Roman Empire	
Owner has the  Augustus trait
Unlocks the Restore Imperial Province casus belli
Reconquering historical provinces of the Roman Empire provides additional bonuses
Roads to Power Eastern Roman Empire	
Byzantine Empire
Any historical empire held when the decision was taken
Byzantion	Cleave the Empire	Owner has the  Augustus trait
Roads to Power Western Roman Empire	
Italia
Any historical empire held when the decision was taken
Roma	Cleave the Empire	Owner has the  Augustus trait
Khans of the Steppe Khaganate	
Amur
Andong
Khazaria
Mongolia
Siberia
Tartaria
Turan
Volga-Ural
Kirghiz Khanate in 867
Kara Khitai in 1178
Carpathia if steppes were expanded into Eastern Balkans
Russia if steppes were expanded into Northern or Southern Russia
Byzantine Empire if steppes were expanded into Caucasus
Persia if steppes were expanded into Persia
No	Reform the Great Khaganate	Additional empires are not added if the Expand the Steppes decision is taken after the hegemony has been created
